[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtriggered a critical security violation: a file path traversal vulnerability. The [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msanitizer detected that the Tika untar logic attempted to write extracted files to [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39ma path outside the intended extraction directory.[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Issue outline  [0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  During an interactive fuzzing run, the `TikaAppUntarringFuzzer` invoked the [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mApache Tika CLI untarring routine [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`org.apache.tika.cli.TikaUntar.main`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. Jazzer’s [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`FilePathTraversal` sanitizer flagged a critical security issue when the fuzzer [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minput caused an archive entry to be written to a traversal path [0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[35m/tmp/[0m[95mexpander-tmp[0m[39m*[0m[35m/output/q/r/[0m[95mjazzer-traversal[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Vulnerability type  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  The issue is classified as a file path traversal vulnerability. The sanitizer [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mraised `com.code_intelligence.jazzer.api.FuzzerSecurityIssueCritical: File path [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtraversal`.[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Important observations  [0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The fuzzer harness sets up environment variables and calls [0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[35m/out/[0m[95mTikaAppUntarringFuzzer[0m[39m -[0m[33mruns[0m[39m=[0m[1;36m100[0m[39m [0m[35m/[0m[95mtestcase[0m[39m`.  [0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • Jazzer logs show extensive bytecode instrumentation of both the fuzz harness [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`com.example.TikaAppUntarringFuzzer`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and the Tika/Commons-Compress classes [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g.,[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`TarArchiveInputStream`, `TikaUntar`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The sanitizer’s stack trace pinpoints `FilePathTraversal.checkPath` being [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minvoked from `org.apache.tika.cli.TikaUntar.main`.  [0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The crash reproducer is generated as a Java test case [0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`Crash_9689beed6cdf68af6291a23a8a117186272d1e5b.java`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, identifying the exact [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpayload that triggers the traversal.[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Code areas to investigate  [0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. `org.apache.tika.cli.TikaUntar.main` – the entry point for unpacking tar [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39marchives and handling extraction paths.  [0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. Commons-Compress tar-processing classes [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`TarArchiveInputStream`, [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`TarArchiveEntry`, `TarUtils`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and the logic that maps archive entries to file [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msystem paths.  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. Any path-sanitization or directory-restriction code within Tika or the [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mextraction harness [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`TikaAppUntarringFuzzer.parseOne`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. Commons-IO utilities used for file creation and I/O operations [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`FileUtils`, `PathUtils`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to see how they handle relative paths and symlinks.[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe fuzz harness itself is only the entry point and not the root cause; a review of[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mTika’s untar implementation and related utility methods is needed to understand how[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39muntrusted archive entries can lead to path traversal.[0m                               [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe initial issue arose when the jazzer-based fuzzer exercised the Tika CLI’s untar[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfunctionality and triggered a `FuzzerSecurityIssueCritical` for file path [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtraversal. The patch added normalization of the extraction directory and a check to[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreject entries whose resolved paths lie outside the target directory, throwing an [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`IOException` in those cases. After applying the patch, the fuzzer still [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcrashes—now with a generic `java.io.IOException: Entry is outside of the target [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdir`—indicating the path-traversal check fired but remains an unhandled exception [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthat causes a crash.[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Initial Issue  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - A jazzer fuzzing run of `TikaAppUntarringFuzzer` on [0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`org.apache.tika.cli.TikaUntar` reported a security sanitizer alert:  [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     `FuzzerSecurityIssueCritical: File path traversal: [0m[35m/tmp/.../[0m[95mjazzer-traversal[0m[39m` [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The sanitizer pipeline detected that an archive entry’s file name led to a [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpath outside the intended output directory.  [0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The crash stack trace pointed to [0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`com.code_intelligence.jazzer.sanitizers.FilePathTraversal.checkPath` invoked from [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`TikaUntar.main`.[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Important Observations in the Initial Issue  [0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The fuzzer harness invoked `TikaUntar.main` with two arguments: the input [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39marchive and the target directory.  [0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No pre-validation of the archive entry names was performed, so entries like [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`..[0m[35m/../[0m[95mjazzer-traversal[0m[39m` escaped the extraction directory.  [0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Jazzer’s sanitizers intercepted the unsafe path and raised a security issue [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrather than letting the code handle it.[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Patch Attempt  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Modified `TikaUntar.main` to normalize and absolutize the extraction [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdirectory:  [0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```java[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     Path extractDir = [0m[1;35mPaths.get[0m[1;39m([0m[39margs[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.toAbsolutePath[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Added a guard before writing each file entry:  [0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```java[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     Path target = [0m[1;35mextractDir.resolve[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mtae.getName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35mtarget.startsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[39mextractDir[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                          [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1120[0m[39m:                [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m being a CLI program messages should go to the stderr too[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1121[0m[39m:                [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1122[0m[39m:                String msg = [0m[1;35mString.format[0m[1;39m([0m[39mLocale.ROOT, [0m[32m"Ignoring unexpected [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32mexception trying to save embedded file %s [0m[32m([0m[32m%s[0m[32m)[0m[32m"[0m[39m, name, [0m[1;35me.getMessage[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1123[0m[39m:                [0m[1;35mLOG.warn[0m[1;39m([0m[39mmsg, e[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1124[0m[39m:            [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Reapply and preserve the directory‐normalization and path traversal guard [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mintroduced in the last patch:[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Compute `extractDir` as  [0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     `[0m[1;35mPaths.get[0m[1;39m([0m[39margs[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.toAbsolutePath[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - For each entry, resolve and normalize the target path and check  [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     `if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35mtarget.startsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[39mextractDir[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` → throw or signal a traversal.[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Prevent per-entry `IOException` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mespecially those raised by the traversal guard[0m[1;39m)[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfrom bubbling out of `main`, which currently causes the fuzzer harness to treat [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthem as fatal crashes. Instead, handle these exceptions in-line per entry, log a [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnon-fatal warning, and continue processing subsequent entries:[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Surround the file‐write logic inside the extraction loop with a try‐catch [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mblock:[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```java[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     while [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mtae = [0m[1;35mtais.getNextEntry[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m != null[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mtae.isFile[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             try [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                 Path target = [0m[1;35mextractDir.resolve[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mtae.getName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                 if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35mtarget.startsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[39mextractDir[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                     throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Entry is outside of the target dir: "[0m[39m +[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mtae.getName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                 [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                 [0m[1;35mFiles.createDirectories[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mtarget.getParent[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                 [0m[1;35mFiles.write[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtarget, [0m[1;35mtais.readAllBytes[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m catch [0m[1;39m([0m[39mIOException e[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                 [0m[1;35mSystem.err.println[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Warning: ignoring entry '"[0m[39m + [0m[1;35mtae.getName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m + [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32m"': "[0m[39m + [0m[1;35me.getMessage[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                 [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m continue with the next entry[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Do not change the signature of `main`; all IOExceptions related to bad entries[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mare caught internally.[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Justification:[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Aligns `TikaUntar` with the non-fatal‐on‐error behavior already employed in [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`TikaCLI.parseEmbedded`, where embedded‐file write failures are caught, logged, and[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mskipped.[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Ensures that malicious or malformed entries [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., path‐traversal attempts[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtrigger only warnings rather than a non-zero exit status and a fuzzer crash.[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Preserves existing functionality for valid entries and still enforces the [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msecurity guard against traversal.[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Side‐effects & mitigation:[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - All legitimate filesystem I/O errors [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., disk full, permission denied[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mduring entry extraction will now be logged and skipped rather than aborting the [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprocess. This matches CLI semantics but may hide some severe conditions. If certain[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mI/O failures must be considered fatal, catch and rethrow only the specific [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexceptions to retain a non-zero exit code.[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Uniformly using `System.err.println` for warnings ensures compatibility [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwithout adding new logging dependencies.[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. No changes are needed to the fuzzer harness, test suites, or external [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdependencies. This patch solely modifies `TikaUntar.main` in `tika-app` and upholds[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe same harness‐triggered code paths.  [0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
